&lt;ul&gt;

&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-110-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.1.0 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated PayTo endpoints to v1 instead of v1.0&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added account_identification_type_code to Amend Mandate request&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated clearing value for attribute payment_execute_not_before_time on Amend Mandate request   &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated Amend Mandate attribute descriptions to indicate more clearly which attributes can be cleared and which ones cannot&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added hyper-links between schema models and PayTo Webhook API&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-104-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.4 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated Amend Mandate examples  &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Removed &lt;strong&gt;payment_initiator_information&lt;/strong&gt; from Create Mandate request&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-103-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.3 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated Amend Mandate examples  &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated REGEX for &lt;strong&gt;uetr&lt;/strong&gt; must be UUID v4&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated REGEX for &lt;strong&gt;request_id&lt;/strong&gt; must be 36 characters&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-102-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.2 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added Amend Mandate operation.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-101-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.1 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated the conditional rules which apply to the creation of mandates specifically new DDRs and migrated DDRs.  &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added Create Mandate example payloads.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added link to PayID information page.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated descriptions from &amp;quot;Payee&amp;quot; to &amp;quot;Biller&amp;quot;. &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added required scope for each API operation.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>Fileactive PayTo API provides consumers the ability to</p>
<ul>
<li>Create a Mandate</li>
<li>Amend a Mandate</li>
<li>Change a Mandate Status</li>
<li>Get Mandate Details</li>
<li>Create a Mandated Payment Initiation Request (MPIR)</li>
<li>Create a PayTo Query Resolution</li>
</ul>
<p>Payloads are to be encrypted and signed prior to transmitting.</p>
<p><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/event-codes#payto-api-event-codes">PayTo API Event Codes</a> </p>
<h4 id="release-110-changes">Release 1.1.0 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Updated PayTo endpoints to v1 instead of v1.0</li>
<li>Added account_identification_type_code to Amend Mandate request</li>
<li>Updated clearing value for attribute payment_execute_not_before_time on Amend Mandate request   </li>
<li>Updated Amend Mandate attribute descriptions to indicate more clearly which attributes can be cleared and which ones cannot</li>
<li>Added hyper-links between schema models and PayTo Webhook API</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="release-104-changes">Release 1.0.4 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Updated Amend Mandate examples  </li>
<li>Removed <strong>payment_initiator_information</strong> from Create Mandate request</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="release-103-changes">Release 1.0.3 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Updated Amend Mandate examples  </li>
<li>Updated REGEX for <strong>uetr</strong> must be UUID v4</li>
<li>Updated REGEX for <strong>request_id</strong> must be 36 characters</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="release-102-changes">Release 1.0.2 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Added Amend Mandate operation.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="release-101-changes">Release 1.0.1 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Updated the conditional rules which apply to the creation of mandates specifically new DDRs and migrated DDRs.  </li>
<li>Added Create Mandate example payloads.</li>
<li>Added link to PayID information page.</li>
<li>Updated descriptions from &quot;Payee&quot; to &quot;Biller&quot;. </li>
<li>Added required scope for each API operation.</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></div><div id="tag/Authorisation" data-section-id="tag/Authorisation" class="sc-eDLKkx hNzKJC"><div class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h1 class="sc-fsYfdN clXmGs"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Authorisation" aria-label="tag/Authorisation"></a>Authorisation</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hLQSwg jSgyLg"><div class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM redoc-markdown " html="&lt;p&gt;Operations related to authentication &amp;amp; authorisation.&lt;/p&gt;
"><p>Operations related to authentication &amp; authorisation.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/Authorisation/operation/auth" data-section-id="tag/Authorisation/operation/auth" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/auth" id="operation/auth" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Authorisation/operation/auth" aria-label="tag/Authorisation/operation/auth"></a>Obtain authorisation token<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;ANZ use OAuth 2.0 to authenticate inbound token requests, a bearer token is returned as a response which is then used to authorise against ANZ resources&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>ANZ use OAuth 2.0 to authenticate inbound token requests, a bearer token is returned as a response which is then used to authorise against ANZ resources</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG">(<span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>OAuth2</i></span>) </span></div></div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-gYrqIg hJSqDi">application/x-www-form-urlencoded</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH sc-jnlcPO itHPsH ciWJhv gcZOqF">required</div></h5><div html="&lt;p&gt;Information and examples of Auth request body&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>Information and examples of Auth request body</p>

" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Production Environment</p>
</div><div tabindex="0" role="button"><div class="sc-lkDHyp etvaCd"><span>https://api.fileactive.anzgcis.com</span>/v1.0/auth</div></div></div></div></div><div><h3 class="sc-kFCroH klfnyk"> <!-- -->Response samples<!-- --> </h3><div class="sc-cyZbeP jSWvqu" data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="tab-success react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-0" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-1" tabindex="0" data-rttab="true">200</li><li class="tab-error" role="tab" id="react-tabs-2" aria-selected="false" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-3" data-rttab="true">default</li></ul><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-1" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-0"><div><div class="sc-cPtzlb jBjImi"><span class="sc-bCvmQg gzGSal">Content type</span><div class="sc-dQmiwx kmXPkl">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-hVcFVo jeLSWq"><div class="sc-cSxRuM fOJBdW"><div class="sc-gjLLEI kJEmUb"><button><div class="sc-jdHILj krcPXE">Copy</div></button></div><div class="sc-iKOmoZ WVNwY sc-jMbVJB DqFKH"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="obj collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="property token string">"expires_in"</span>: <span class="token number">3600</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="property token string">"token_type"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;Bearer&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="property token string">"access_token"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;eaaa13ee-b596-a8cc-b9d4-f778f8bb9377&quot;</span></div></li></ul><span class="token aria-labelledby="react-tabs-2"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/Mandate" data-section-id="tag/Mandate" class="sc-eDLKkx hNzKJC"><div class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h1 class="sc-fsYfdN clXmGs"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Mandate" aria-label="tag/Mandate"></a>Mandate</h1></div></div><div class="sc-hLQSwg jSgyLg"><div class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM redoc-markdown " html="&lt;p&gt;Operations related to mandates.&lt;/p&gt;
"><p>Operations related to mandates.</p>
</div></div></div><div id="tag/Mandate/operation/createMandate" data-section-id="tag/Mandate/operation/createMandate" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/createMandate" id="operation/createMandate" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Mandate/operation/createMandate" aria-label="tag/Mandate/operation/createMandate"></a>Create a new mandate.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to create a new mandate in the MMS. A mandate is always created by the Payment Initiator. If the Establishment Scheme for the mandate is &amp;#39;AUPM&amp;#39; then the mandate will be created bilaterally, otherwise it will be created unilaterally. A unilaterally created mandate will have initial status &amp;#39;Active&amp;#39; and version &amp;#39;1&amp;#39; whereas a bilaterally created mandate will have initial status &amp;#39;Created&amp;#39; and version &amp;#39;0&amp;#39;. A bilaterally created mandate can only become &amp;#39;Active&amp;#39; when the Debtor confirms the creation of the mandate, at which moment its&amp;#39; version will also increase to &amp;#39;1&amp;#39;. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;A bilateral mandate creation will automatically expire after a fixed time period if the creation action is not completed, declined or recalled. Expiry of a mandate creation will result in the mandate status being set to &amp;#39;Cancelled&amp;#39;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request. The processing outcome of the request will be delivered via the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Mandate&quot;&gt;PayTo Webhook API - Mandate Processing Outcomes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this API:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;EstablishmentSchemeRule1: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;creditor_information&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;EstablishmentSchemeRule2: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;additional_information&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be populated with the BECS User Id of the Initiating Party.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;EstablishmentSchemeRule3: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is  equal to &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;resolution_requested_by&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be absent.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;ValidityEndDateRule1: If &lt;code&gt;validity_end_date&lt;/code&gt; is present then &lt;code&gt;automatic_extension_indicator&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be &amp;#39;false&amp;#39;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;ValidityEndDateRule2: If &lt;code&gt;validity_end_date&lt;/code&gt; is &lt;strong&gt;not&lt;/strong&gt; present then &lt;code&gt;automatic_extension_indicator&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be &amp;#39;true&amp;#39;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to create a new mandate in the MMS. A mandate is always created by the Payment Initiator. If the Establishment Scheme for the mandate is &#39;AUPM&#39; then the mandate will be created bilaterally, otherwise it will be created unilaterally. A unilaterally created mandate will have initial status &#39;Active&#39; and version &#39;1&#39; whereas a bilaterally created mandate will have initial status &#39;Created&#39; and version &#39;0&#39;. A bilaterally created mandate can only become &#39;Active&#39; when the Debtor confirms the creation of the mandate, at which moment its&#39; version will also increase to &#39;1&#39;. </p>
<p>A bilateral mandate creation will automatically expire after a fixed time period if the creation action is not completed, declined or recalled. Expiry of a mandate creation will result in the mandate status being set to &#39;Cancelled&#39;.</p>
<p>The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request. The processing outcome of the request will be delivered via the <strong><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Mandate">PayTo Webhook API - Mandate Processing Outcomes</a></strong>.</p>
<p>The following rules apply to this API:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>EstablishmentSchemeRule1: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>creditor_information</code> <strong>must</strong> be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>EstablishmentSchemeRule2: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>additional_information</code> <strong>must</strong> be populated with the BECS User Id of the Initiating Party.</p>
</li>
<li><p>EstablishmentSchemeRule3: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is  equal to &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>resolution_requested_by</code> <strong>must</strong> be absent.</p>
</li>
<li><p>ValidityEndDateRule1: If <code>validity_end_date</code> is present then <code>automatic_extension_indicator</code> <strong>must</strong> be &#39;false&#39;.</p>
</li>
<li><p>ValidityEndDateRule2: If <code>validity_end_date</code> is <strong>not</strong> present then <code>automatic_extension_indicator</code> <strong>must</strong> be &#39;true&#39;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG">(<span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>bearerAuth</i></span>) </span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Correlation-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Correlation-Id</span></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">71d6fb19-7515-40dc-b045-e17550b67600</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Optional correlation ID provided by the data consumer that should be reflected back in the response headers. Can be used for reporting and logging.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Optional correlation ID provided by the data consumer that should be reflected back in the response headers. Can be used for reporting and logging.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Message-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Message-Id</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">71d6fb19-7515-40dc-b045-e17550b67600</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="priority" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">priority</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->NotificationPriority1Code<!-- -->) </span></div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;ATTENDED&quot;</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;UNATTENDED&quot;</span> </div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Priority (attended/unattended) to be included in any generated notification. This value does not affect the priority for processing within the MMS. It may, depending on topic configuration, influence which topic any generated notification is sent to.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Priority (attended/unattended) to be included in any generated notification. This value does not affect the priority for processing within the MMS. It may, depending on topic configuration, influence which topic any generated notification is sent to.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">Request Body schema: <span class="sc-gYrqIg hJSqDi">application/json</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH sc-jnlcPO itHPsH ciWJhv gcZOqF">required</div></h5><div html="&lt;p&gt;Secured resource to create a mandate in the MMS.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;Examples are reflective of unencrypted payload. &lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>Secured resource to create a mandate in the MMS.</p>

data-rttabs="true"><ul class="react-tabs__tab-list" role="tablist"><li class="tab-error react-tabs__tab--selected" role="tab" id="react-tabs-6" aria-selected="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-7" tabindex="0" data-rttab="true">400</li><li class="tab-error" role="tab" id="react-tabs-8" aria-selected="false" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-9" data-rttab="true">500</li><li class="tab-error" role="tab" id="react-tabs-10" aria-selected="false" aria-disabled="false" aria-controls="react-tabs-11" data-rttab="true">default</li></ul><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-7" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-6"><div><div class="sc-cPtzlb jBjImi"><span class="sc-bCvmQg gzGSal">Content type</span><div class="sc-dQmiwx kmXPkl">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-hVcFVo jeLSWq"><div class="sc-cSxRuM fOJBdW"><div class="sc-gjLLEI kJEmUb"><button><div class="sc-jdHILj krcPXE">Copy</div></button><button> Expand all </button><button> Collapse all </button></div><div class="sc-iKOmoZ WVNwY sc-jMbVJB DqFKH"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="obj collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="property token string">"status"</span>: <button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="obj collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"severity"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;Fatal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"code"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;EC004_001&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"text"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;Internal Server Error, please contact support.&quot;</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-9" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-8"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-11" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-10"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/Mandate/operation/changeMandateStatus" data-section-id="tag/Mandate/operation/changeMandateStatus" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/changeMandateStatus" id="operation/changeMandateStatus" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Mandate/operation/changeMandateStatus" aria-label="tag/Mandate/operation/changeMandateStatus"></a>Change the status of a mandate.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to change the status of a mandate. A status change is always performed as a unilateral operation. The status can only be changed when the mandate is currently active or suspended. Releasing a suspended mandate can only be performed by the party that suspended the mandate. A status change can be applied when there is a pending amendment and also when porting is in progress. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Upon successful status change the mandate version number will be incremented. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Any notification triggered by this operation will have priority UNATTENDED. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request. The processing outcome of the request will be delivered via the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Mandate&quot;&gt;PayTo Webhook API - Mandate Processing Outcomes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;.  &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this API:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;ChangeAndReasonCodeRule1: When &lt;code&gt;change&lt;/code&gt; is equal to value &amp;#39;CNCL&amp;#39; or &amp;#39;SUSP&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;reason_code&lt;/code&gt; must be present.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to change the status of a mandate. A status change is always performed as a unilateral operation. The status can only be changed when the mandate is currently active or suspended. Releasing a suspended mandate can only be performed by the party that suspended the mandate. A status change can be applied when there is a pending amendment and also when porting is in progress. </p>
<p>Upon successful status change the mandate version number will be incremented. </p>
<p>Any notification triggered by this operation will have priority UNATTENDED. </p>
<p>The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request. The processing outcome of the request will be delivered via the <strong><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Mandate">PayTo Webhook API - Mandate Processing Outcomes</a></strong>.  </p>
<p>The following rules apply to this API:</p>
<ul>
<li>ChangeAndReasonCodeRule1: When <code>change</code> is equal to value &#39;CNCL&#39; or &#39;SUSP&#39; then <code>reason_code</code> must be present.</li>
</ul>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG">(<span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>bearerAuth</i></span>) </span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="mandateId" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">mandateId</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">^[a-f0-9]{12}1[a-f0-9]{3}[89ab][a-f0-9]{15}$</span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;ID of mandate whose status is to be updated.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>ID of mandate whose status is to be updated.</p>

class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-15" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-14"><div><div class="sc-cPtzlb jBjImi"><span class="sc-bCvmQg gzGSal">Content type</span><div class="sc-dQmiwx kmXPkl">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-hVcFVo jeLSWq"><div class="sc-cSxRuM fOJBdW"><div class="sc-gjLLEI kJEmUb"><button><div class="sc-jdHILj krcPXE">Copy</div></button><button> Expand all </button><button> Collapse all </button></div><div class="sc-iKOmoZ WVNwY sc-jMbVJB DqFKH"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="obj collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="property class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"severity"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;Fatal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"code"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;EC004_001&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"text"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;Internal Server Error, please contact support.&quot;</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-17" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-16"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-19" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-18"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/Mandate/operation/amendMandate" data-section-id="tag/Mandate/operation/amendMandate" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/amendMandate" id="operation/amendMandate" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Mandate/operation/amendMandate" aria-label="tag/Mandate/operation/amendMandate"></a>Amend mandate<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to amend an existing mandate. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The MMS will determine if the amendment is to be performed unilaterally or bilaterally based on the party role of the caller and the fields being amended. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;When applied unilaterally then the amendment will be applied immediately. &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;When applied bilaterally, the amendment will remain pending until it is completed or declined by the Payer, or until it is recalled by the Biller, or until it expires.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Only a single bilateral amendment can be pending per mandate at any time. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Any attempt to amend a mandate that must be performed bilaterally where there is already a pending amendment will fail. However, unilateral amendments may still be performed where a pending amendment exists. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;For a unilateral amendment the changes will only be applied to the mandate if the amendment does not invalidate the mandate integrity. &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;For a bilateral amendment, the integrity of the changes will be verified when the amendment request is received and again at the moment that the action is confirmed.         &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;The rules determining the integrity of the mandate are defined in the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api#tag/Mandate/operation/createMandate&quot;&gt;PayTo API - Create Mandate&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;A mandate amendment will automatically expire after a fixed time period if the amendment is not completed, declined or recalled. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;For a bilateral amendment the mandate version number will only be incremented when the amendment action is successfully completed.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request. The processing outcome of the request will be delivered via the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Mandate&quot;&gt;PayTo Webhook API - Mandate Processing Outcomes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to amend an existing mandate. </p>
<p>The MMS will determine if the amendment is to be performed unilaterally or bilaterally based on the party role of the caller and the fields being amended. </p>
<ul>
<li>When applied unilaterally then the amendment will be applied immediately. </li>
<li>When applied bilaterally, the amendment will remain pending until it is completed or declined by the Payer, or until it is recalled by the Biller, or until it expires.</li>
</ul>
<p>Only a single bilateral amendment can be pending per mandate at any time. </p>
<p>Any attempt to amend a mandate that must be performed bilaterally where there is already a pending amendment will fail. However, unilateral amendments may still be performed where a pending amendment exists. </p>
<ul>
<li>For a unilateral amendment the changes will only be applied to the mandate if the amendment does not invalidate the mandate integrity. </li>
<li>For a bilateral amendment, the integrity of the changes will be verified when the amendment request is received and again at the moment that the action is confirmed.         </li>
<li>The rules determining the integrity of the mandate are defined in the <strong><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api#tag/Mandate/operation/createMandate">PayTo API - Create Mandate</a></strong>.</li>
</ul>
<p>A mandate amendment will automatically expire after a fixed time period if the amendment is not completed, declined or recalled. </p>
<p>For a bilateral amendment the mandate version number will only be incremented when the amendment action is successfully completed.</p>
<p>The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request. The processing outcome of the request will be delivered via the <strong><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Mandate">PayTo Webhook API - Mandate Processing Outcomes</a></strong>.</p>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG">(<span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>bearerAuth</i></span>) </span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">path<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="mandateId" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">mandateId</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">^[a-f0-9]{12}1[a-f0-9]{3}[89ab][a-f0-9]{15}$</span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;ID of mandate to be amended.&lt;/p&gt;

aria-labelledby="react-tabs-30"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-33" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-32"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-35" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-34"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-37" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-36"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-39" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-38"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-41" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-40"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-43" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-42"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/MPIR" data-section-id="tag/MPIR" class="sc-eDLKkx hNzKJC"><div class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h1 class="sc-fsYfdN clXmGs"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/MPIR" aria-label="tag/MPIR"></a>MPIR</h1></div></div></div><div id="tag/MPIR/operation/createMPIR" data-section-id="tag/MPIR/operation/createMPIR" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/createMPIR" id="operation/createMPIR" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/MPIR/operation/createMPIR" aria-label="tag/MPIR/operation/createMPIR"></a>Create a new MPIR.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to create a new mandated payment initiation request (MPIR). The underlying mandate &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be in an &amp;#39;Active&amp;#39; state. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the MPIR processing outcome of the request. The MPIR processing outcome will be delivered via the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/MPIR&quot;&gt;PayTo Webhook API - MPIR Processing Outcomes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this API:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;MPSUserSchemeRule1: &lt;code&gt;mps_user_id&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be the owner of the provided &lt;code&gt;mandate_identification&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;InstructedAmountSchemeRule1: &lt;code&gt;instructed_amount&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; not exceed the maximum amount specified in the associated mandate &lt;code&gt;mandate_identification&lt;/code&gt; &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CreditorDetailsSchemeRule1: &lt;code&gt;creditor_information&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be present where not provided on the mandate.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CreditorDetailsSchemeRule2: &lt;code&gt;creditor_information&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;should&lt;/strong&gt; not be present where provided on the mandate.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CreditorDetailsSchemeRule3: If &lt;code&gt;creditor_information&lt;/code&gt; is provided and is also available on the mandate then details &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be exactly the same.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to create a new mandated payment initiation request (MPIR). The underlying mandate <strong>must</strong> be in an &#39;Active&#39; state. </p>
<p>The initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the MPIR processing outcome of the request. The MPIR processing outcome will be delivered via the <strong><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/MPIR">PayTo Webhook API - MPIR Processing Outcomes</a></strong>. </p>
<p>The following rules apply to this API:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>MPSUserSchemeRule1: <code>mps_user_id</code> <strong>must</strong> be the owner of the provided <code>mandate_identification</code></p>
</li>
<li><p>InstructedAmountSchemeRule1: <code>instructed_amount</code> <strong>must</strong> not exceed the maximum amount specified in the associated mandate <code>mandate_identification</code> </p>
</li>
<li><p>CreditorDetailsSchemeRule1: <code>creditor_information</code> <strong>must</strong> be present where not provided on the mandate.</p>
</li>
<li><p>CreditorDetailsSchemeRule2: <code>creditor_information</code> <strong>should</strong> not be present where provided on the mandate.</p>
</li>
<li><p>CreditorDetailsSchemeRule3: If <code>creditor_information</code> is provided and is also available on the mandate then details <strong>must</strong> be exactly the same.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG">(<span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>bearerAuth</i></span>) </span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Correlation-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Correlation-Id</span></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">71d6fb19-7515-40dc-b045-e17550b67600</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Optional correlation ID provided by the data consumer that should be reflected back in the response headers. Can be used for reporting and logging.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Optional correlation ID provided by the data consumer that should be reflected back in the response headers. Can be used for reporting and logging.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Message-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Message-Id</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">71d6fb19-7515-40dc-b045-e17550b67600</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="priority" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">priority</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->NotificationPriority1Code<!-- -->) </span></div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Enum<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;ATTENDED&quot;</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;UNATTENDED&quot;</span> </div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;MPIR Priority (attended/unattended). Urgency or order of importance that the originator would like the recipient of the payment instruction to apply to the processing of the payment instruction. class="react-tabs__tab-panel react-tabs__tab-panel--selected" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-47" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-46"><div><div class="sc-cPtzlb jBjImi"><span class="sc-bCvmQg gzGSal">Content type</span><div class="sc-dQmiwx kmXPkl">application/json</div></div><div class="sc-hVcFVo jeLSWq"><div class="sc-cSxRuM fOJBdW"><div class="sc-gjLLEI kJEmUb"><button><div class="sc-jdHILj krcPXE">Copy</div></button><button> Expand all </button><button> Collapse all </button></div><div class="sc-iKOmoZ WVNwY sc-jMbVJB DqFKH"><div class="redoc-json"><code><button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="obj collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable "><span class="property token string">"status"</span>: <button class="collapser" aria-label="collapse"></button><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="ellipsis"></span><ul class="obj collapsible"><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"severity"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;Fatal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="hoverable collapsed"><span class="property token string">"code"</span>: <span class="token string">&quot;EC004_001&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span></div></li><li><div class="token punctuation">}</span></div></li></ul><span class="token punctuation">}</span></code></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-49" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-48"></div><div class="react-tabs__tab-panel" role="tabpanel" id="react-tabs-51" aria-labelledby="react-tabs-50"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="tag/Query" data-section-id="tag/Query" class="sc-eDLKkx hNzKJC"><div class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h1 class="sc-fsYfdN clXmGs"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Query" aria-label="tag/Query"></a>Query</h1></div></div></div><div id="tag/Query/operation/queryResolution" data-section-id="tag/Query/operation/queryResolution" class="sc-eDLKkx cSNAXN"><div data-section-id="operation/queryResolution" id="operation/queryResolution" class="sc-iBdnpw fsPUig"><div class="sc-hLQSwg gikxZY"><h2 class="sc-qZrbh lmuvuv"><a class="sc-csKJxZ fNhImz" href="#tag/Query/operation/queryResolution" aria-label="tag/Query/operation/queryResolution"></a>PayTo query resolution.<!-- --> </h2><div class="sc-eYFTNc dZbpPF"><div html="&lt;p&gt;The purpose of this operation is to provide a resolution to a PayTo query raised by the &lt;strong&gt;Payer&amp;#39;s&lt;/strong&gt; Financial Institution. Queries are delivered via the &lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Query&quot;&gt;PayTo Webhook API - PayTo Queries&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;.  &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this API: &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CaseDecisionSchemeRule1: &lt;code&gt;case_decision&lt;/code&gt; = &lt;strong&gt;ACPT&lt;/strong&gt; then &lt;code&gt;reject_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;return_transaction_identification&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;should not&lt;/strong&gt; be provided. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CaseDecisionSchemeRule2: &lt;code&gt;case_decision&lt;/code&gt; = &lt;strong&gt;FINO&lt;/strong&gt; then &lt;code&gt;reject_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;return_transaction_identification&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;should not&lt;/strong&gt; be provided.  &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CaseDecisionSchemeRule3: &lt;code&gt;case_decision&lt;/code&gt; = &lt;strong&gt;PEND&lt;/strong&gt; then &lt;code&gt;reject_reason_code&lt;/code&gt;, &lt;code&gt;return_transaction_identification&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;should not&lt;/strong&gt; be provided. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;CaseDecisionSchemeRule4: &lt;code&gt;case_decision&lt;/code&gt; = &lt;strong&gt;RJCT&lt;/strong&gt; then &lt;code&gt;reject_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be provided.   &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;RejectReasonSchemeRule1: &lt;code&gt;reject_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; = &lt;strong&gt;ARDT&lt;/strong&gt; then &lt;code&gt;return_transaction_identification&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be provided.  &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;RejectReasonSchemeRule2: &lt;code&gt;reject_reason_code&lt;/code&gt; = &lt;strong&gt;CUST&lt;/strong&gt; then &lt;code&gt;return_transaction_identification&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must not&lt;/strong&gt; be provided.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>The purpose of this operation is to provide a resolution to a PayTo query raised by the <strong>Payer&#39;s</strong> Financial Institution. Queries are delivered via the <strong><a href="https://anz-insto.github.io/fileactive/api/payto-api-webhook#tag/Query">PayTo Webhook API - PayTo Queries</a></strong>.  </p>
<p>The following rules apply to this API: </p>
<ul>
<li><p>CaseDecisionSchemeRule1: <code>case_decision</code> = <strong>ACPT</strong> then <code>reject_reason_code</code> and <code>return_transaction_identification</code> <strong>should not</strong> be provided. </p>
</li>
<li><p>CaseDecisionSchemeRule2: <code>case_decision</code> = <strong>FINO</strong> then <code>reject_reason_code</code> and <code>return_transaction_identification</code> <strong>should not</strong> be provided.  </p>
</li>
<li><p>CaseDecisionSchemeRule3: <code>case_decision</code> = <strong>PEND</strong> then <code>reject_reason_code</code>, <code>return_transaction_identification</code> <strong>should not</strong> be provided. </p>
</li>
<li><p>CaseDecisionSchemeRule4: <code>case_decision</code> = <strong>RJCT</strong> then <code>reject_reason_code</code> <strong>must</strong> be provided.   </p>
</li>
<li><p>RejectReasonSchemeRule1: <code>reject_reason_code</code> = <strong>ARDT</strong> then <code>return_transaction_identification</code> <strong>must</strong> be provided.  </p>
</li>
<li><p>RejectReasonSchemeRule2: <code>reject_reason_code</code> = <strong>CUST</strong> then <code>return_transaction_identification</code> <strong>must not</strong> be provided.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div></div><div class="sc-jPpdYo kZYbVV"><div class="sc-drMgrp bizpoY"><h5 class="sc-irLvIq sc-jSUdEz cnGhhy gpGSCt">Authorizations:</h5><svg class="sc-eTNRI jFDiGT" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></div><div class="sc-cZpZpK kkdamf"><span class="sc-hNDLBw esvqYG">(<span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>apiKeyAuth</i></span><span class="sc-kGLCbq kHXFc"><i>bearerAuth</i></span>) </span></div></div><div><h5 class="sc-irLvIq cnGhhy">header<!-- --> Parameters</h5><table class="sc-hIPBNq kuUpel"><tbody><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Correlation-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Correlation-Id</span></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">71d6fb19-7515-40dc-b045-e17550b67600</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Optional correlation ID provided by the data consumer that should be reflected back in the response headers. Can be used for reporting and logging.&lt;/p&gt;

</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="X-Message-Id" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">X-Message-Id</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->UUID<!-- -->) </span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ejCKsa itHPsH gSlWhd">[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{...</span><button class="sc-faxByu kKHJHX">Show pattern</button></div> <div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Example:<!-- --> </span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">71d6fb19-7515-40dc-b045-e17550b67600</span></div><div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Duplicate check using point to point reference, as assigned by the instructing party, and sent to the next party in the chain to unambiguously identify the message&lt;/p&gt;

</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="priority" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">priority</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->NotificationPriority2Code<!-- -->) </span></div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS itHPsH"> <!-- -->Value<!-- -->:</span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-ldgOGP itHPsH cRxwgg">&quot;UNATTENDED&quot;</span> </div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Priority (attended/unattended) to be included in any generated notification. This must be a Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID). This UUID must be unique amongst all request_ids passed to this end-point by the same MPS User. If a request is encountered with a request ID that has previously been used then a duplicate check will be performed by comparing the digest of the current request with the digest of the previous request. If the digests match then the details of the previous mandate amendment will be returned. If the digests do not match then an HTTP 409 will be returned.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Request UUID that identifies the mandate amendment operation to be performed. This must be a Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID). This must be a Universally Unique IDentifier (UUID). This UUID must be unique amongst all request_ids passed to this end-point by the same MPS User. </div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="automatic_extension_indicator" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">automatic_extension_indicator</span><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">boolean</span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Automatic renewal of a mandate arrangement at the end of the defined period (period start through period end).&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Automatic renewal of a mandate arrangement at the end of the defined period (period start through period end).</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="debtor_information" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy sc-jiaSqj cqoAxn hfWKVF gIkRoy"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><button aria-label="expand debtor_information"><span class="property-name">debtor_information</span><svg class="sc-eTNRI jIsRbK" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">object</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->MandatePartyInformation1Debtor<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Information concerning the debtor party identified in the mandate. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this structure:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;AccountIdentificationRule1: If &lt;code&gt;account_identification_type_code&lt;/code&gt; is equal to value &amp;#39;ALIA&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;account_alias_type_code&lt;/code&gt;  and &lt;code&gt;account_alias_identification&lt;/code&gt; must be present, and &lt;code&gt;account_identification&lt;/code&gt; must be absent.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;AccountIdentificationRule2: If &lt;code&gt;account_identification_type_code&lt;/code&gt; is equal to value &amp;#39;BBAN&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;account_identification&lt;/code&gt; must be present and start with BSB (bank-state-branch), and &lt;code&gt;account_alias_type_code&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;account_alias_identification&lt;/code&gt; must be absent.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;AccountIdentificationRule3: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to value &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;account_identification_type_code&lt;/code&gt; must be equal to value &amp;#39;BBAN&amp;#39;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Information concerning the debtor party identified in the mandate. </p>
<p>The following rules apply to this structure:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>AccountIdentificationRule1: If <code>account_identification_type_code</code> is equal to value &#39;ALIA&#39; then <code>account_alias_type_code</code>  and <code>account_alias_identification</code> must be present, and <code>account_identification</code> must be absent.</p>
</li>
<li><p>AccountIdentificationRule2: If <code>account_identification_type_code</code> is equal to value &#39;BBAN&#39; then <code>account_identification</code> must be present and start with BSB (bank-state-branch), and <code>account_alias_type_code</code> and <code>account_alias_identification</code> must be absent.</p>
</li>
<li><p>AccountIdentificationRule3: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to value &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>account_identification_type_code</code> must be equal to value &#39;BBAN&#39;.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="creditor_information" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy sc-jiaSqj cqoAxn hfWKVF gIkRoy"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><button aria-label="expand creditor_information"><span class="property-name">creditor_information</span><svg class="sc-eTNRI jIsRbK" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">object</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->MandatePartyInformation1Creditor<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Information concerning the creditor party identified in the mandate.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this structure:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;CreditorPartyTypeRule1: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;party_type&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;must&lt;/strong&gt; be present.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Information concerning the creditor party identified in the mandate.</p>
<p>The following rules apply to this structure:</p>
<ul>
<li>CreditorPartyTypeRule1: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>party_type</code> <strong>must</strong> be present.</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="payment_information" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy sc-jiaSqj cqoAxn hfWKVF gIkRoy"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><button aria-label="expand payment_information"><span class="property-name">payment_information</span><svg class="sc-eTNRI jIsRbK" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button><div class="sc-gUjWJS sc-eKzvBH itHPsH ciWJhv">required</div></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">object</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->MandatePaymentInformation1<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Set of characteristics detailing mandate payment information.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property descriptions&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;payment_frequency&lt;/strong&gt; - Regularity with which instructions are to be created and processed.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;payment_amount_type&lt;/strong&gt; - Identifies the mandate payment arrangement.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;first_payment_amount&lt;/strong&gt; - Amount different from the payment amount, as it includes the costs associated with the first debited amount.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;last_payment_amount&lt;/strong&gt; - Last payment amount different  to the payment amount.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;amount&lt;/strong&gt; - Fixed amount to be debited from the debtor&amp;#39;s account.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;maximum_amount&lt;/strong&gt; - Maximum amount that may be paid from the debtor&amp;#39;s account, per instruction.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The following rules apply to this structure:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountTypeRule1: If &lt;code&gt;payment_amount_type&lt;/code&gt; code is equal to value &amp;#39;FIXE&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;amount&lt;/code&gt; must be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountTypeRule2: If &lt;code&gt;payment_amount_type&lt;/code&gt; code is equal to value &amp;#39;BALN&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;amount&lt;/code&gt; must be present AND (&lt;code&gt;first_payment amount&lt;/code&gt; OR &lt;code&gt;last_payment amount&lt;/code&gt;) must be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountTypeRule3: If &lt;code&gt;payment_amount_type&lt;/code&gt; code is equal to value &amp;#39;USGB&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;maximum_amount&lt;/code&gt; must be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountTypeRule4: If &lt;code&gt;payment_amount_type&lt;/code&gt; code is equal to value &amp;#39;VARI&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;maximum_amount&lt;/code&gt; must be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;FirstPaymentDateRule1: &lt;code&gt;first_payment_date&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be before &lt;code&gt;validity_start_date&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;FirstPaymentDateRule2: &lt;code&gt;first_payment_date&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be after &lt;code&gt;validity_end_date&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;FirstPaymentDateRule3: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;first_payment_date&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;LastPaymentDateRule1: &lt;code&gt;last_payment_date&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be before &lt;code&gt;validity_start_date&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;LastPaymentDateRule2: &lt;code&gt;last_payment_date&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be after &lt;code&gt;validity_end_date&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;FrequencyInTermsRule1: Both &lt;code&gt;count_per_period&lt;/code&gt; AND &lt;code&gt;point_in_time&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountRule1: &lt;code&gt;amount&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; exceed &lt;code&gt;maximum_amount&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountRule2: &lt;code&gt;first_payment_amount&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; exceed &lt;code&gt;maximum_amount&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountRule3: &lt;code&gt;last_payment_amount&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; exceed &lt;code&gt;maximum_amount&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;PaymentAmountRule4: If &lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39; then &lt;code&gt;first_payment_amount&lt;/code&gt; &lt;strong&gt;cannot&lt;/strong&gt; be present.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Set of characteristics detailing mandate payment information.</p>
<p><strong>Property descriptions</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>payment_frequency</strong> - Regularity with which instructions are to be created and processed.</li>
<li><strong>payment_amount_type</strong> - Identifies the mandate payment arrangement.</li>
<li><strong>first_payment_amount</strong> - Amount different from the payment amount, as it includes the costs associated with the first debited amount.</li>
<li><strong>last_payment_amount</strong> - Last payment amount different  to the payment amount.</li>
<li><strong>amount</strong> - Fixed amount to be debited from the debtor&#39;s account.</li>
<li><strong>maximum_amount</strong> - Maximum amount that may be paid from the debtor&#39;s account, per instruction.</li>
</ul>
<p>The following rules apply to this structure:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>PaymentAmountTypeRule1: If <code>payment_amount_type</code> code is equal to value &#39;FIXE&#39; then <code>amount</code> must be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountTypeRule2: If <code>payment_amount_type</code> code is equal to value &#39;BALN&#39; then <code>amount</code> must be present AND (<code>first_payment amount</code> OR <code>last_payment amount</code>) must be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountTypeRule3: If <code>payment_amount_type</code> code is equal to value &#39;USGB&#39; then <code>maximum_amount</code> must be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountTypeRule4: If <code>payment_amount_type</code> code is equal to value &#39;VARI&#39; then <code>maximum_amount</code> must be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>FirstPaymentDateRule1: <code>first_payment_date</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be before <code>validity_start_date</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>FirstPaymentDateRule2: <code>first_payment_date</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be after <code>validity_end_date</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>FirstPaymentDateRule3: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>first_payment_date</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>LastPaymentDateRule1: <code>last_payment_date</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be before <code>validity_start_date</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>LastPaymentDateRule2: <code>last_payment_date</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be after <code>validity_end_date</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>FrequencyInTermsRule1: Both <code>count_per_period</code> AND <code>point_in_time</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be present.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountRule1: <code>amount</code> <strong>cannot</strong> exceed <code>maximum_amount</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountRule2: <code>first_payment_amount</code> <strong>cannot</strong> exceed <code>maximum_amount</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountRule3: <code>last_payment_amount</code> <strong>cannot</strong> exceed <code>maximum_amount</code>.</p>
</li>
<li><p>PaymentAmountRule4: If <code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to &#39;MGCR&#39; then <code>first_payment_amount</code> <strong>cannot</strong> be present.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="additional_information" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy cqoAxn hfWKVF"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><span class="property-name">additional_information</span></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">string</span><span> <span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-cmfnrN itHPsH iOjfOC"> <!-- -->[ 1 .. 140 ] characters<!-- --> </span></span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Additional information, in free text form, to complement the mandate information.
Specifies a character string with a maximum length of 140 characters.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Where the Mandate is a Migrated DDR (&lt;code&gt;establishment_scheme&lt;/code&gt; is equal to value &amp;#39;MGCR&amp;#39;), this field is used to denote the existing BECS User ID of the Initiating Party.
The format is //BECSID/xxxxxx where xxxxxx is the BECS DD User ID used by the Initiating Party in an existing DDR arrangement.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Additional information, in free text form, to complement the mandate information.
Specifies a character string with a maximum length of 140 characters.</p>
<p>Where the Mandate is a Migrated DDR (<code>establishment_scheme</code> is equal to value &#39;MGCR&#39;), this field is used to denote the existing BECS User ID of the Initiating Party.
The format is //BECSID/xxxxxx where xxxxxx is the BECS DD User ID used by the Initiating Party in an existing DDR arrangement.</p>

A mandate is always created by the Payment Initiator. If the Establishment Scheme for the mandate is 'AUPM' then the mandate will be created bilaterally, otherwise it will be created unilaterally. A unilaterally created mandate will have initial status 'Active' and version '1' whereas a bilaterally created mandate will have initial status 'Created' and version '0'. A bilaterally created mandate can only become 'Active' when the Debtor confirms the creation of the mandate, at which moment its' version will also increase to '1'. \n\nA bilateral mandate creation will automatically expire after a fixed time period if the creation action is not completed, declined or recalled. Expiry of a mandate creation will result in the mandate status being set to 'Cancelled'.\n\nThe initial API response indicates if ANZ has accepted or rejected the request, not the processing outcome of the request.
